          <div data-target="readme-toc.content" class="Box-body px-5 pb-5">
            <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-instant-neural-graphics-primitives-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#instant-neural-graphics-primitives-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Instant Neural Graphics Primitives <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/workflows/CI/badge.svg"><img src="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/workflows/CI/badge.svg" alt="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-this-is-a-forked-windows-installation-tutorial-and-the-main-codes-will-not-be-updated" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#this-is-a-forked-windows-installation-tutorial-and-the-main-codes-will-not-be-updated"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>This is a forked Windows Installation Tutorial and the main codes will not be updated</h2>
<p dir="auto">Follow this YouTube <a href="https://youtu.be/kq9xlvz73Rg" rel="nofollow">tutorial</a> to understand the installation process more easily and if you have any questions feel free to join my <a href="https://discord.gg/sE8R7e45MV" rel="nofollow">discord</a> and ask there.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/fox.gif"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/fox.gif" height="342" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/robot5.gif"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/robot5.gif" height="342" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Ever wanted to train a NeRF model of a fox in under 5 seconds? Or fly around a scene captured from photos of a factory robot? Of course you have!</p>
<p dir="auto">Here you will find an implementation of four <strong>neural graphics primitives</strong>, being neural radiance fields (NeRF), signed distance functions (SDFs), neural images, and neural volumes.
In each case, we train and render a MLP with multiresolution hash input encoding using the <a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/tiny-cuda-nn">tiny-cuda-nn</a> framework.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Instant Neural Graphics Primitives with a Multiresolution Hash Encoding</strong><br>
<a href="https://tom94.net" rel="nofollow">Thomas Müller</a>, <a href="https://research.nvidia.com/person/alex-evans" rel="nofollow">Alex Evans</a>, <a href="https://research.nvidia.com/person/christoph-schied" rel="nofollow">Christoph Schied</a>, <a href="https://research.nvidia.com/person/alex-keller" rel="nofollow">Alexander Keller</a><br>
<em><a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2201.05989" rel="nofollow">arXiv:2201.05989 [cs.CV]</a>, Jan 2022</em><br>
<strong>[ <a href="https://nvlabs.github.io/instant-ngp" rel="nofollow">Project page</a> ] [ <a href="https://nvlabs.github.io/instant-ngp/assets/mueller2022instant.pdf" rel="nofollow">Paper</a> ] [ <a href="https://nvlabs.github.io/instant-ngp/assets/mueller2022instant.mp4" rel="nofollow">Video</a> ] [ <a href="https://nvlabs.github.io/instant-ngp/assets/mueller2022instant.bib" rel="nofollow">BibTeX</a> ]</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">For business inquiries, please visit our website and submit the form: <a href="https://www.nvidia.com/en-us/research/inquiries/" rel="nofollow">NVIDIA Research Licensing</a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-requirements" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Requirements</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>An <strong>NVIDIA GPU</strong>; tensor cores increase performance when available. All shown results come from an RTX 3090.</li>
<li>Python ver: 3.9.*</li>
<li><a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/visualstudio/releases/2019/history" rel="nofollow">Visual Studio Community 2019</a> (Latest the best, ~8GB) Below are the install requirements
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151634222-6ac236c9-5fa7-4762-9144-73e50959cb65.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151634222-6ac236c9-5fa7-4762-9144-73e50959cb65.png" alt="image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
<li><strong><a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/cuda-downloads?target_os=Windows&amp;target_arch=x86_64&amp;target_version=10&amp;target_type=exe_network" rel="nofollow">CUDA</a> v11.6</strong>. You can check ur CUDA version via <code>nvcc --version</code> in any prompt and if it's not CUDA11.6, refer to <a href="https://github.com/bycloudai/SwapCudaVersionWindows">this</a> to swap/install the correct version.</li>
<li>On some machines, <code>pyexr</code> refuses to install via <code>pip</code>. This can be resolved by installing OpenEXR from <a href="https://www.lfd.uci.edu/~gohlke/pythonlibs/#openexr" rel="nofollow">here</a>. See later.</li>
<li>This installation tutorial will be using Anaconda. Download anaconda prompt <a href="https://www.anaconda.com/products/individual" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/optix" rel="nofollow">OptiX</a> 7.3 or higher</strong> for faster mesh SDF training. You need to either login or join to obtain the installer. Set the system environment variables <code>OptiX_INSTALL_DIR</code> to the installation directory if it is not discovered automatically. Should look like this: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151631220-7a934f5c-c299-41ab-a44e-184e2dc142b9.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151631220-7a934f5c-c299-41ab-a44e-184e2dc142b9.png" alt="image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-compilation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compilation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Compilation</h2>
<p dir="auto">copy these files <code>C:\Program Files\NVIDIA GPU Computing Toolkit\CUDA\v11.6\extras\visual_studio_integration\MSBuildExtensions</code>
to here <code>C:\Program Files (x86)\Microsoft Visual Studio\2019\Community\MSBuild\Microsoft\VC\v160\BuildCustomizations</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>cd</code> into a directory that you want to download the codes at. Eg. <code>cd F:\Tutorial\ngp\</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Begin by cloning this repository and all its submodules using the following command (if you don't have git, download <a href="https://git-scm.com/download/win" rel="nofollow">here</a> and add to path):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ git clone --recursive https://github.com/nvlabs/instant-ngp
$ cd instant-ngp"><pre>$ git clone --recursive https://github.com/nvlabs/instant-ngp
$ <span class="pl-c1">cd</span> instant-ngp</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">if your python is not 3.9 (check with command <code>python --version</code>) then you need to run the following command to get it to ver 3.9.*</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="conda install python=3.9"><pre><code>conda install python=3.9
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Then, open <strong>Developer Command Prompt</strong>, you can find this in your search bar.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151631759-ff8538ab-74c6-4c7b-962e-d7b097e819db.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151631759-ff8538ab-74c6-4c7b-962e-d7b097e819db.png" alt="image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Then <code>cd</code> to where you cloned your repository so you are in its root folder <code>/instant-ng/</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cmake . -B build
cmake --build build --config RelWithDebInfo -j 16"><pre>cmake <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -B build
cmake --build build --config RelWithDebInfo -j 16</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If the any of these build fails, please consult <a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp#troubleshooting-compile-errors">this list of possible fixes</a> before opening an issue.</p>
<p dir="auto">If automatic GPU architecture detection fails, (as can happen if you have multiple GPUs installed), set the  <code>TCNN_CUDA_ARCHITECTURES</code> enivonment variable for the GPU you would like to use. The following table lists the values for common GPUs. If your GPU is not listed, consult <a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/cuda-gpus" rel="nofollow">this exhaustive list</a>.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>RTX 30X0</th>
<th>A100</th>
<th>RTX 20X0</th>
<th>TITAN V / V100</th>
<th>GTX 10X0 / TITAN Xp</th>
<th>GTX 9X0</th>
<th>K80</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>86</td>
<td>80</td>
<td>75</td>
<td>70</td>
<td>61</td>
<td>52</td>
<td>37</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-interactive-training-and-rendering-on-custom-image-sets" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#interactive-training-and-rendering-on-custom-image-sets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Interactive Training and Rendering on Custom Image Sets</h2>
<p dir="auto">Install <a href="https://github.com/colmap/colmap/releases/tag/3.7">COLMAP</a>, I used ver 3.7</p>
<p dir="auto">Add it to your system environment variables at Environment Variables &gt; System Variables Path &gt; Edit environment variable</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151633058-e45f9220-c417-4249-aff3-09d29c1a4e9b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/29135514/151633058-e45f9220-c417-4249-aff3-09d29c1a4e9b.png" alt="image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">open anaconda prompt, if you don't have you don't have you can get it <a href="https://www.anaconda.com/products/individual" rel="nofollow">here</a>
<code>cd</code> into isntant-ngp as root</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="conda create -n ngp python=3.9
conda activate ngp
pip install -r requirements.txt"><pre>conda create -n ngp python=3.9
conda activate ngp
pip install -r requirements.txt</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">if <code>pyexr</code> cannot be installed via <code>pip install pyexr</code>, download <a href="https://www.lfd.uci.edu/~gohlke/pythonlibs/#openexr" rel="nofollow">OpenEXR‑1.3.2‑cp39‑cp39‑win_amd64.whl</a> and move it to your root folder. Then you can run:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install OpenEXR-1.3.2-cp39-cp39-win_amd64.whl"><pre><code>pip install OpenEXR-1.3.2-cp39-cp39-win_amd64.whl
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Place your custom image set under <code>data/&lt;image_set_name&gt;</code></p>
<p dir="auto">Get <code>transform.json</code> from the following command. Insert your path to your images at <code>&lt;image/path&gt;</code></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python scripts/colmap2nerf.py --colmap_matcher exhaustive --run_colmap --aabb_scale 16 --images &lt;image/path&gt;"><pre>python scripts/colmap2nerf.py --colmap_matcher exhaustive --run_colmap --aabb_scale 16 --images <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>image/path<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>transform.json</code> will be generated at the root folder, drag and drop it into your <code>data/&lt;image_set_name&gt;</code> folder.</p>
<p dir="auto">You have to reorganize the folder structure due to how <code>transforms.json</code> is created...</p>
<p dir="auto">For example:</p>
<p dir="auto">File Structure <strong>BEFORE</strong> generating transform.json</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="📂instant-ngp/ # this is root
├── 📂data/
│	├── 📂toy_truck/
│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_001.jpg
│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_002.jpg
│	│	│...
│   │...
│..."><pre><code>📂instant-ngp/ # this is root
├── 📂data/
│	├── 📂toy_truck/
│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_001.jpg
│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_002.jpg
│	│	│...
│   │...
│...
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">File Structure <strong>AFTER</strong> generating transform.json</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="📂instant-ngp/ # this is root
├── 📂data/
│	├── 📂toy_truck/
│	│	├── 📜transforms.json/
│	│	├── 📂data/
│	│	│	├── 📂toy_truck/
│	│	│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_001.jpg
│	│	│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_002.jpg
│	│	│	│	│...
│	│	│	│...
│	│	│...
│	│...
│..."><pre><code>📂instant-ngp/ # this is root
├── 📂data/
│	├── 📂toy_truck/
│	│	├── 📜transforms.json/
│	│	├── 📂data/
│	│	│	├── 📂toy_truck/
│	│	│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_001.jpg
│	│	│	│	├── 📜toy_truck_002.jpg
│	│	│	│	│...
│	│	│	│...
│	│	│...
│	│...
│...
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note: adjusting the <code>"aabb_scale"</code> inside <code>transform.json</code> can reduce load on GPU VRAM. The lower the value the less intensive it'll be.</p>
<p dir="auto">Finally, to run instant-ngp:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;path_to_your_ngp&gt;\instant-ngp\build\testbed.exe --scene data/&lt;image_set_name&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>path_to_your_ngp<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span><span class="pl-cce">\i</span>nstant-ngp<span class="pl-cce">\b</span>uild<span class="pl-cce">\t</span>estbed.exe --scene data/<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>image_set_name<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">eg.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="C:\user\user\download\instant-ngp\build\testbed.exe --scene data/toy_truck"><pre><code>C:\user\user\download\instant-ngp\build\testbed.exe --scene data/toy_truck
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">And it should launch the GUI and everything amazing with it</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-rendering-custom-camera-path" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rendering-custom-camera-path"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Rendering custom camera path</h2>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>May need to install more dependencies. Install <code>pip install tqdm scipy pillow opencv-python</code>, <code>conda install -c conda-forge ffmpeg</code>, might be needed in the conda virtual environment. Refer to installation of <code>pyexr</code> above in the installation section if you didn't install that too.</li>
<li>Train any image set like above.</li>
<li>After you have reached a point that you are satisfied with your training, save a Snapshot on the GUI. (one of the tabs &amp; no need to edit the path &amp; the name)</li>
<li>Find another GUI called camera path, it'll play hide and seek with you but it is there so find that window.</li>
<li>The GUI is so well made, if you know how to use any 3D engine, it's really similar. Add camera path will give you a new angle of the camera.</li>
<li>After you have finished adding your camera points, save the camera path. (no need to edit the path &amp; the name)</li>
<li>Render the path with the following command:</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python scripts/render.py --scene &lt;scene_path&gt; --n_seconds &lt;seconds&gt; --fps &lt;fps&gt; --render_name &lt;name&gt; --width &lt;resolution_width&gt; --height &lt;resolution_height&gt;
"><pre>python scripts/render.py --scene <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>scene_path<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> --n_seconds <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>seconds<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> --fps <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>fps<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> --render_name <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>name<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> --width <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>resolution_width<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> --height <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>resolution_height<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">eg.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python scripts/render.py --scene data/toy --n_seconds 5 --fps 60 --render_name test --width 1920 --height 1080"><pre>python scripts/render.py --scene data/toy --n_seconds 5 --fps 60 --render_name <span class="pl-c1">test</span> --width 1920 --height 1080</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Your video will be saved at root. You might have to play around with the <code>fps</code> and <code>n_seconds</code> to speed up or slow down. I couldn't get it accurately because of the lack of information and this is the best I could come up with. To be honest, this is only a short-term solution too, since the author has promised to publish an official one. So stay tuned!</p>
<p dir="auto">And my fork edits end here.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-interactive-training-and-rendering" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#interactive-training-and-rendering"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Interactive training and rendering</h2>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/testbed.png"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/testbed.png" width="100%" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">This codebase comes with an interactive testbed that includes many features beyond our academic publication:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Additional training features, such as extrinsics and intrinsics optimization.</li>
<li>Marching cubes for <code>NeRF-&gt;Mesh</code> and <code>SDF-&gt;Mesh</code> conversion.</li>
<li>A spline-based camera path editor to create videos.</li>
<li>Debug visualizations of the activations of every neuron input and output.</li>
<li>And many more task-specific settings.</li>
<li>See also our <a href="https://nvlabs.github.io/instant-ngp/assets/mueller2022instant.mp4" rel="nofollow">one minute demonstration video of the tool</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-nerf-fox" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#nerf-fox"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>NeRF fox</h3>
<p dir="auto">One test scene is provided in this repository, using a small number of frames from a casually captured phone video:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/nerf/fox"><pre>instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/nerf/fox</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/fox.png"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/fox.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, download any NeRF-compatible scene (e.g. <a href="https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/1JDdLGDruGNXWnM1eqY1FNL9PlStjaKWi" rel="nofollow">from the NeRF authors' drive</a>).
Now you can run:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/nerf_synthetic/lego/transforms_train.json"><pre>instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/nerf_synthetic/lego/transforms_train.json</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For more information about preparing datasets for use with our NeRF implementation, please see <a href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/nerf_dataset_tips.md">this document</a>.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-sdf-armadillo" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#sdf-armadillo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>SDF armadillo</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/sdf/armadillo.obj"><pre>instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/sdf/armadillo.obj</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/armadillo.png"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/armadillo.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-image-of-einstein" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#image-of-einstein"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Image of Einstein</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/image/albert.exr"><pre>instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/image/albert.exr</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/albert.png"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/albert.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">To reproduce the gigapixel results, download, for example, <a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/trevor_dobson_inefekt69/29314390837" rel="nofollow">the Tokyo image</a> and convert it to <code>.bin</code> using the <code>scripts/image2bin.py</code> script. This custom format improves compatibility and loading speed when resolution is high. Now you can run:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/image/tokyo.bin"><pre>instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --scene data/image/tokyo.bin</pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-volume-renderer" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#volume-renderer"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Volume Renderer</h3>
<p dir="auto">Download the <a href="https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/1SuycSAOSG64k2KLV7oWgyNWyCvZAkafK?usp=sharing" rel="nofollow">nanovdb volume for the Disney cloud</a>, which is derived <a href="https://disneyanimation.com/data-sets/?drawer=/resources/clouds/" rel="nofollow">from here</a> (<a href="https://media.disneyanimation.com/uploads/production/data_set_asset/6/asset/License_Cloud.pdf" rel="nofollow">CC BY-SA 3.0</a>).</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --mode volume --scene data/volume/wdas_cloud_quarter.nvdb"><pre>instant-ngp$ ./build/testbed --mode volume --scene data/volume/wdas_cloud_quarter.nvdb</pre></div>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/blob/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/cloud.png"><img src="/bycloudai/instant-ngp-Windows/raw/a526ced31b2842a99d84adaa962687133e4e4a19/docs/assets_readme/cloud.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-python-bindings" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#python-bindings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Python bindings</h2>
<p dir="auto">To conduct controlled experiments in an automated fashion, all features from the interactive testbed (and more!) have Python bindings that can be easily instrumented.
For an example of how the <code>./build/testbed</code> application can be implemented and extended from within Python, see <code>./scripts/run.py</code>, which supports a superset of the command line arguments that <code>./build/testbed</code> does.</p>
<p dir="auto">Happy hacking!</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-troubleshooting-compile-errors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#troubleshooting-compile-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Troubleshooting compile errors</h2>
<p dir="auto">Before investigating further, make sure all submodules are up-to-date and try compiling again.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="instant-ngp$ git submodule sync --recursive
instant-ngp$ git submodule update --init --recursive"><pre>instant-ngp$ git submodule sync --recursive
instant-ngp$ git submodule update --init --recursive</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If <strong>instant-ngp</strong> still fails to compile, update CUDA as well as your compiler to the latest versions you can install on your system. It is crucial that you update <em>both</em>, as newer CUDA versions are not always compatible with earlier compilers and vice versa.
If your problem persists, consult the following table of known issues.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Problem</th>
<th>Resolution</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>CMake error:</strong> No CUDA toolset found / CUDA_ARCHITECTURES is empty for target "cmTC_0c70f"</td>
<td><strong>Windows:</strong> the Visual Studio CUDA integration was not installed correctly. Follow <a href="https://github.com/mitsuba-renderer/mitsuba2/issues/103#issuecomment-618378963" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/mitsuba-renderer/mitsuba2/issues/103/hovercard">these instructions</a> to fix the problem without re-installing CUDA. (<a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/18" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/18/hovercard">#18</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td></td>
<td><strong>Linux:</strong> Environment variables for your CUDA installation are probably incorrectly set. You may work around the issue using <code>cmake . -B build -DCMAKE_CUDA_COMPILER=/usr/local/cuda-&lt;your cuda version&gt;/bin/nvcc</code> (<a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/28" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/28/hovercard">#28</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>CMake error:</strong> No known features for CXX compiler "MSVC"</td>
<td>Reinstall Visual Studio &amp; make sure you run CMake from a developer shell. (<a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/21" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/21/hovercard">#21</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Compile error:</strong> undefined references to "cudaGraphExecUpdate" / identifier "cublasSetWorkspace" is undefined</td>
<td>Update your CUDA installation (which is likely 11.0) to 11.3 or higher. (<a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/34" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/34/hovercard">#34</a> <a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/41" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/41/hovercard">#41</a> <a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/42" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/42/hovercard">#42</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Compile error:</strong> too few arguments in function call</td>
<td>Update submodules with the above two <code>git</code> commands. (<a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/37" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/37/hovercard">#37</a> <a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/52" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/52/hovercard">#52</a>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Python error:</strong> No module named 'pyngp'</td>
<td>It is likely that CMake did not detect your Python installation and therefore did not build <code>pyngp</code>. Check CMake logs to verify this. If <code>pyngp</code> was built in a different folder than <code>instant-ngp/build</code>, Python will be unable to detect it and you have to supply the full path to the import statement. (<a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/43" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/43/hovercard">#43</a>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">If you cannot find your problem in the table, please feel free to <a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/instant-ngp/issues/new">open an issue</a> and ask for help.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-thanks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#thanks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Thanks</h2>
<p dir="auto">Many thanks to <a href="https://research.nvidia.com/person/jonathan-tremblay" rel="nofollow">Jonathan Tremblay</a> and <a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/blog/author/atao/" rel="nofollow">Andrew Tao</a> for testing early versions of this codebase and to Arman Toorians and Saurabh Jain for the factory robot dataset.
We also thank <a href="https://github.com/grey-area">Andrew Webb</a> for noticing that one of the prime numbers in the spatial hash was not actually prime; this has been fixed since.</p>
<p dir="auto">This project makes use of a number of awesome open source libraries, including:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/NVlabs/tiny-cuda-nn">tiny-cuda-nn</a> for fast CUDA MLP networks</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/syoyo/tinyexr">tinyexr</a> for EXR format support</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/tinyobjloader/tinyobjloader">tinyobjloader</a> for OBJ format support</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/nothings/stb">stb_image</a> for PNG and JPEG support</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/ocornut/imgui">Dear ImGui</a> an excellent immediate mode GUI library</li>
<li><a href="https://eigen.tuxfamily.org/index.php?title=Main_Page" rel="nofollow">Eigen</a> a C++ template library for linear algebra</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/pybind/pybind11">pybind11</a> for seamless C++ / Python interop</li>
<li>and others! See the <code>dependencies</code> folder.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Many thanks to the authors of these brilliant projects!</p>
